However, with the high prices of gas we've been experiencing over the years, I decided to try FVF, since their prices are usually lower than anyone. I also visit ARCO, since they're always cheaper than the other big companies, but they only take cash, or charge a ATM fee. Staff is friendly and inviting, this is of course a reflection of the management. As a coffee drinker, if they do not have the dark roast coffee on standby, they will gladly brew up a batch, albeit 7 minute wait.
Great hang out for the cyclist! Observation front, corner patio is environmentally relaxing accompanied with a artsy water fountain to mimic river sounds. Plenty of room for a group.
As for the automobiliest seeking parking on peak hours, terrible! You have the wannabe Shitpotle Mexican restaurant sharing the the same parking lot. Don't even try to enter! Park across the street at the empty bank.</Review>

< Text>
Go to this Macy's and ask for SHIRLEY Toolsie!!!

I walked in to the ladies'  department yesterday, lost and fashion-challenged, looking for an outfit for an interview.  She listened to me, asked a couple of specific questions, and then pulled a PERFECT outfit for me.  I tried it on and it was MAGICAL.  In 2 minutes she had completely understood and gotten me an adorable, hip and trendy dress and sweater/jacket set that looked good on my body, was appropriate for the situation, and even reflected my personality!  (And it was 25% off!)

Believe me, I was knocked out.  When I came out of the dressing room, other customers kept complimenting me and asking Shirley for help for themselves.  She is a miracle worker.

I ended up buying two more dresses she picked out that fit like a glove and are really cute.  I  couldn't be happier.  I will go to this Macy's and seek out Shirley for every fashion decision I make from now on!

Thank you, Shirley!!!!<//Text>

I brought my Volt in for the replacement of an inside wheel well cover. There was also separation of the front quarter panel from the bumper and damage to areas where the bumper and panel connected.
